\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_scheduled\_transactions()}{get\_scheduled\_transactions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1testing_1_1base__tester_a3d7501a4597b6536451d1f791641b3e0} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classfc_1_1vector}{vector}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_aa85a3b49b3b219d1e3840567579e7e63}{transaction\+\_\+id\+\_\+type}} $>$ sysio\+::testing\+::base\+\_\+tester\+::get\+\_\+scheduled\+\_\+transactions (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

These transaction IDs represent transactions available in the head chain state as scheduled or otherwise generated transactions.

calling push\+\_\+scheduled\+\_\+transaction with these IDs will remove the associated transaction from the chain state IFF it succeeds or objectively fails

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
